⚠️[ TRIAL FUND (BONUS) USAGE & PROFIT GUIDE ]
The rewards provided in this event are issued as "Trial Funds." These are designed to provide you with additional margin and cover costs, allowing you to trade more aggressively.

• Usage for Margin & Fees: Trial funds can be used as margin to open larger positions. They are also automatically used to offset trading fees and cover potential trading losses, protecting your real capital.
• Fully Withdrawable Profits: While the trial fund itself cannot be withdrawn, 100% of the profits generated from trading with these funds are yours to keep and can be withdrawn at any time.
• Proportional Deduction: When you open a position, the system uses your real capital and the trial fund proportionally. If a loss occurs, the trial fund shares the burden, significantly reducing your personal risk.

⚠️[ TRIAL FUND (BONUS) USAGE & PROFIT GUIDE ]
The rewards provided in this event are issued as "Trial Funds." These are designed to provide you with additional margin and cover costs, allowing you to trade more aggressively.

• Usage for Margin & Fees: Trial funds can be used as margin to open larger positions. They are also automatically used to offset trading fees and cover potential trading losses, protecting your real capital.
• Fully Withdrawable Profits: While the trial fund itself cannot be withdrawn, 100% of the profits generated from trading with these funds are yours to keep and can be withdrawn at any time.
• Proportional Deduction: When you open a position, the system uses your real capital and the trial fund proportionally. If a loss occurs, the trial fund shares the burden, significantly reducing your personal risk.

⚠️ [ TRIAL FUND (BONUS) USAGE & PROFIT GUIDE ]
The rewards distributed during the Deposit Carnival are issued as "Trial Funds." These funds act as a powerful tool for both novice and professional traders to enhance their market strategy.

• Usage for Margin & Fees: Trial funds are versatile assets that can be used as margin for opening new positions. They are also automatically applied to offset trading fees and funding fees, ensuring that your actual balance remains untouched for longer.
• Risk Mitigation: If you encounter trading losses, the trial funds act as a buffer to cover those losses, effectively protecting your deposited capital from initial market volatility.
• Withdrawable Profits: While the trial fund itself is used for trading purposes within the platform and cannot be withdrawn, any and all profits generated from successful trades made with these funds are fully withdrawable by the user.

🆘**Bonus Usage Rules and Guidelines**

1. Large Positions (Position ≥ 500 USDT)

Practical Example:
Suppose you have a principal of 2,000 USDT and a bonus of 500 USDT. You decide to open a position worth 1,300 USDT.

Initial Allocation: 500 USDT (Bonus) + 800 USDT (Principal).

In Case of a 1,000 USDT Loss: Approximately 384 USDT will be deducted from the bonus, while the remaining 116 USDT will expire automatically upon closing.

In Case of a 600 USDT Profit: Part of the transaction fees will be covered by the bonus, but the entire remaining bonus balance will be forfeited once the trade is finalized.

2. Small Positions (Position < 500 USDT)

Practical Example:
Suppose you have a principal of 2,000 USDT and a bonus of 500 USDT. You decide to open a position worth 500 USDT.

Initial Allocation: 250 USDT (Bonus Used) + 250 USDT (Principal Used).

Remaining Buffer: 250 USDT of the bonus is held in reserve and preserved.

In Case of a 300 USDT Loss: 150 USDT is deducted from the active bonus and 150 USDT from the principal. While the 100 USDT remaining from the "active" portion expires, your 250 USDT reserve remains fully available for your next trade.

[2026-02-13 01:42] msg_id=412
레드터틀 증정금 작업에 대한 생각 2026  

기본 전제 : 이벤트 헌팅 금지, 다계정 금지.

우선 여기저기서 증정금에 대한 글들이 보이기 시작하면서 거래소 관계자, 국내 자문업체, 다양한분들을 직접 만나고 이벤트시장에 지금까지 참여해 오며 느낀 점을 바탕으로 몇 자 더해본다.

1. 많은 채널이 증정금에 대한 방법론 적인 글을 다루지 않는 이유는 단순히 ‘꿀통이라서 공유하지 않는다’기보다 더 치명적이고 중요한 이유가 존재한다.

2. 실제로 증정금 이벤트 참여는 상승장이든 하락장이든 꾸준히 투입 대비 높은 수익을 가져다주었고, 지금도 그렇다. 1인 참여만으로도 일반 회사원 월급 이상을 벌 수 있다.  
   *예를 들어 최근 Picol 이벤트는 단 이틀 만에 2,000달러의 리워드를 지급했으며, 참여 유저들의 평균 수익은 약 1,300달러(한화 약 200만 원) 수준이었다.

3. 다만 증정금 이벤트에는 강력한 리스크가 많다. 거래소는 헌팅유저,불법행위에 대한 자금 동결, 제재, 미지급, 수수료 문제 등 나열하자면 A4 한 장이 모자랄 정도다.

4. 유저는 자신이 헌팅 유저가 아닌 ‘일반 트레이더’임을 다양한 방식으로, 그리고 적극적+오버해서 어필/증명 해야 한다.

5. “이런 수익이 왜 가능하지? 거래소가 자선단체는 아닐 텐데.”라는 질문에 대한 답은 분명 존재한다. 거래소 역시 이러한 이벤트를 통해 얻는 이익이 있다.

6. “이 증정금 이벤트 시장이 오래가지 못하는 것 아닐까?”라는 질문에 대해서는 장기적인 시계열에서는 우하향할 가능성이 있다고 본다. 그러나 그 시점까지는 아직 시간이 남아 있다고 판단한다.

7. 다만 대한민국 유저들에게 주어진 시간은 2026년 12/31 이전까지라고 본다.

8. 그리고 7번에 대한 돌파구 역시 존재한다.

9. 여러 이유로 모든 것을 직접적으로 말하기는 어렵다. 솔직히 말해 ‘꿀통’인 것도 맞지만, 그보다 더 크고 강력한 이유들이 있다.

10. 증정금 이벤트 시장은 구조적으로 Win-Win이 가능하다.

11. 그래서 일반 유저나 초보자라면 매매를 병행하든, 다양한 이벤트에 적극적으로 참여하든 월급에 준하는 부수익을 최대한 안전하게 가져가길 바란다. 충분히 가능한 일이기 때문이다.


많은 분들이 무엇보다 소중한 자산을 지켜가며 이 시장에 참여하길 바란다.  

레터크루 1기와 2기, 그리고 다양한 멤버들을 만나면서 한 가지 분명히 느낀 점이 있다. 실제로 삶이 바뀌고 다시 희망을 바라보게 되는 순간들을 여러 번 목격했다. 나 역시 그 과정을 지나온 사람이다.  

증정금 이벤트 시장은 결국 인풋과 아웃풋이 정비례한다. 많이 노력하고, 부지런히 참여하는 사람일수록 더 높은 수익을 가져간다.  

조급함보다는 꾸준함으로, 편법보다는 원칙으로 접근하길 바란다. 이 시장은 아직 준비된 사람에게 기회를 주고 있다.

📌 초보분들을 위한 증정금 Q&A (압축)

Q1. 공부 기간은?
A. 초보 → 중수 약 1개월.
혼자 전략 설계까지 약 2개월.
집중도에 따라 차이 있음.

Q2. 적정 시드?
A. 개인차 큼.
보통 1~3만 달러 이내에서 운영.

Q3. 월 수익 가능 범위?
A. 일반 참여자 기준
월 500~1,000만 원 구간은 현실적.
전제는 성실한 참여와 규정 준수.

Q4. 이벤트 1회성인데 지속 수익 가능?
A. 이벤트는 계속 신규 오픈.
신규 거래소, 신규 이벤트, 기존 유저 대상 이벤트 계속있음.

예시)
Phemex, Deepcoin, Ourbit 기존 유저 지속 케어
Picol 오픈 당시 3일 참여 약 $3,000
이벤트는 끊기지 않음.

Q5. 안전한가?
A. 100% 안전 아님.
제 멤버분들 통계상 ~80% 목표달성
~10%는 실수·규정 위반 등으로 손실.
결과는 운이 아니라 운영.꼼꼼함.필요

Q6. 가장 중요한 것?
이벤트 정독, 꼼꼼함필요.
일반 유저임을 강하게증명
리스크에대한 최대한인지
거래소는 헌팅 계정 리스크 관리 철저함.
일반유저로서 오해받지않게 하기.

[2026-03-02 05:10] msg_id=424
📌 증정금N년차의 2월 이벤트 시장에 대한 고찰

최근 이벤트 시장에서 가장 중요한 3가지를 생각해봤습니다.

1.이벤트 해석 & 전략
이벤트 페이지를 반드시 반드시 꼼꼼히 정독해야 합니다.
공지 글을 대략적으로 보고 “이렇게하면 될까나?” 식으로 접근하면 사고가 납니다.
조건, 기간, 보상 구조, 제한 사항까지 스스로 해석하고 질문거리를 정리해야 합니다.

2.리스크 관리 (가장 중요)
이건 100번 말해도 부족합니다.
자금 동결, 계정 제재, 큰 금액 리스크에 걸리면
이벤트 시장에서 사실상 퇴학당할 수도 있습니다.
 
저 또한 수십건의 리스크 사례와 수 년동안 거래소 측과의 대화를 통해서
체화 하였습니다. 그전까지 누가 하나하나 알려주지않았었습니다.

리스크 관리는 경험하기 전까지 배우기 어렵습니다.
경험과 사례, 데이터에서 나오기 때문이죠.
일반 유저가 할 수 있는 최고의 선택은
“항상 리스크를 상정하고 가장 보수적으로 접근하는 것” 입니다.

3.매매 기술
이벤트 시장도 결국 매매가 포함됩니다.
충동매매, 기분매매는 여기서도 동일하게 위험합니다.

대단한 기술이 필요한 건 아닙니다.
자기만의 기준을 만들고
이벤트 구조에 맞게 설정된 매매 원칙만 있어도 충분합니다.
제가 종종 알려드리는 기술들로도 충분하다고봅니다.
각자 반드시 기준을 세우시길 바랍니다.

정리하면
① 이벤트해석
② 리스크 관리
③ 매매 기준

이 세 가지를 제대로 이해해야 오래 갑니다.

최근 유입이 많아진 만큼
기초부터 다시 점검하는 문화가 필요합니다.
아니면 이벤트 시장에 대한 인식이 좋아지지 않을겁니다.

한국 이벤트 시장이
안전하고 건강하게 더 커지길 바랍니다.

🎉 50% Deposit Bonus (Up to 5,000 USDT)

🟢Deepcoin New Membership Link (60%)🟢

https://s.deepcoin.com/sebfcgg

✅Loss Deduction 33%
✅50% Deposit Bonus (Upon Meeting Trading Volume)


📅 Event Period
2026.2.1 ~ 2.28.
 ⁃ One month

✅ Eligibility Requirements
 1. ✨ New registration on Deepcoin Exchange during the event period
 2. 💰 Deposit 1,000 USDT or more
 3. 🚀 Bonus granted for Futures trading
 -  Receive 100 USDT bonus for every 1 BTC futures trading volume, based on 200,000 USDT trading volume per BTC
 4. 💎 Bonus amount varies by deposit and trading volume, up to a maximum of 5,000 USDT
 5. Only users who registered after August 1 are eligible

🔗 How to Participate
 1. Register on Deepcoin Exchange during the event period
 2. Deposit at least 1,000 USDT
 3. Start futures trading (bonus will be issued automatically upon meeting trading volume requirements)
 4. Claim your bonus on the “Reward Page”

⚠️ Important Notes
 • Multiple-account participation is not allowed
 • Accounts flagged for risk control are excluded
 • Only newly registered users are eligible
 • Any withdrawal or fund transfer will result in bonus forfeiture
 • Bonus deduction rate is 33%, applicable to trading fees and losses
 • Trading fee deductions may reduce commission rebates
 • Bonus funds are not eligible for withdrawal
 • Fees are deducted in real time, while losses are settled after position liquidation
 • Loss deductions occur upon bonus expiration, fund transfer, or withdrawal
 • Bonus & fund display:
 • Total Assets = Actual funds + Bonus
 • “Estimated Remaining Bonus” shows the bonus amount only

📜 Event Rules
 1. Users must complete KYC verification to participate. Sub-accounts are not eligible.
 2. Deposits and trades must be completed within the event period and transferred to the Futures Wallet to qualify. Transactions outside the event period will not be counted.
 3. Bonuses can be claimed after meeting deposit and trading requirements. If a withdrawal or fund transfer occurs during the event, the bonus will be reclaimed. Users may requalify by redepositing and meeting the requirements again.
 4. Event deposits are calculated based on net deposits, defined as:
Total deposits during the event (including purchased assets) − total withdrawals during the event
(Internal transfers are excluded from net deposit calculations.)
 5. Only futures trading volume is counted toward the event.
 6. The bonus is valid for 1 year, and the claim period is 30 days. Unclaimed or reclaimed bonuses will not be reissued.
 7. Bonuses can offset 33% of futures trading losses and fees.
 • Example: If 500 USDT in trading fees is incurred at the taker rate,
500 × 33% = 165 USDT will be deducted from the bonus, resulting in an actual fee payment of 335 USDT.
 8. Bonuses are prioritized for real-time fee deductions during trading.
However, final loss offset calculations are conducted after bonus expiration, withdrawal, or fund transfer, based on the net P&L (total profits minus total losses), not at individual position liquidation.
(Fees offset using bonuses are not included in rebate calculations.)
 9. Rewards are automatically distributed to the Reward Center of eligible accounts and must be manually claimed by the user.
 10. Bonuses cannot be withdrawn, transferred, or traded.
 11. When trial funds expire, open positions will be automatically closed and the trial funds will be reclaimed.
Please manage your positions in advance to avoid potential losses.
 12. Deepcoin reserves the right to cancel or reclaim rewards obtained through fraud, illegal activities, or abnormal behavior. Users involved in wash trading, multiple account registration, self-trading, or market manipulation will be disqualified.
 13. Deepcoin reserves the final right of interpretation for this event and may modify, adjust, or cancel the event terms without prior notice.

 4. 💎 Bonus amount varies by deposit and trading volume, up to a maximum of 5,000 USDT
 5. Only users who registered after August 1 are eligible

🔗 How to Participate
 1. Register on Deepcoin Exchange during the event period
 2. Deposit at least 1,000 USDT
 3. Start futures trading (bonus will be issued automatically upon meeting trading volume requirements)
 4. Claim your bonus on the “Reward Page”

⚠️ Important Notes
 • Multiple-account participation is not allowed
 • Accounts flagged for risk control are excluded
 • Only newly registered users are eligible
 • Any withdrawal or fund transfer will result in bonus forfeiture
 • Bonus deduction rate is 33%, applicable to trading fees and losses
 • Trading fee deductions may reduce commission rebates
 • Bonus funds are not eligible for withdrawal
 • Fees are deducted in real time, while losses are settled after position liquidation
 • Loss deductions occur upon bonus expiration, fund transfer, or withdrawal
 • Bonus & fund display:
 • Total Assets = Actual funds + Bonus
 • “Estimated Remaining Bonus” shows the bonus amount only

📜 Event Rules
 1. Users must complete KYC verification to participate. Sub-accounts are not eligible.
 2. Deposits and trades must be completed within the event period and transferred to the Futures Wallet to qualify. Transactions outside the event period will not be counted.
 3. Bonuses can be claimed after meeting deposit and trading requirements. If a withdrawal or fund transfer occurs during the event, the bonus will be reclaimed. Users may requalify by redepositing and meeting the requirements again.
 4. Event deposits are calculated based on net deposits, defined as:
Total deposits during the event (including purchased assets) − total withdrawals during the event
(Internal transfers are excluded from net deposit calculations.)
 5. Only futures trading volume is counted toward the event.
 6. The bonus is valid for 1 year, and the claim period is 30 days. Unclaimed or reclaimed bonuses will not be reissued.
 7. Bonuses can offset 33% of futures trading losses and fees.
 • Example: If 500 USDT in trading fees is incurred at the taker rate,
500 × 33% = 165 USDT will be deducted from the bonus, resulting in an actual fee payment of 335 USDT.
 8. Bonuses are prioritized for real-time fee deductions during trading.
However, final loss offset calculations are conducted after bonus expiration, withdrawal, or fund transfer, based on the net P&L (total profits minus total losses), not at individual position liquidation.
(Fees offset using bonuses are not included in rebate calculations.)
 9. Rewards are automatically distributed to the Reward Center of eligible accounts and must be manually claimed by the user.
 10. Bonuses cannot be withdrawn, transferred, or traded.
 11. When trial funds expire, open positions will be automatically closed and the trial funds will be reclaimed.
Please manage your positions in advance to avoid potential losses.
 12. Deepcoin reserves the right to cancel or reclaim rewards obtained through fraud, illegal activities, or abnormal behavior. Users involved in wash trading, multiple account registration, self-trading, or market manipulation will be disqualified.
 13. Deepcoin reserves the final right of interpretation for this event and may modify, adjust, or cancel the event terms without prior notice.

3. All rewards are paid in the form of trial funds and can be used to deduct margin, trading fees, and funding fees for opening positions.  4. Unauthorized activities, such as self-trading or multi-account cooperative trading, are strictly prohibited, and rewards will be revoked if violated.

 Guide to Bonus Usage Rules
Summary of Key Rules

1️⃣ Position ≥ 500U:
The entire bonus is used; any unused portion is automatically forfeited after liquidation.

2️⃣ Position < 500U:
Partial bonus is used; any unused portion can be used for future trades.

3️⃣ The bonus can only be deducted from losses and fees; it does not apply to profits.

① Position ≥ 500U (Large Position)

System Rules:

Full bonus must be used.

Losses are deducted based on the position ratio. Only fees are deducted as a trial bonus for profits. The remaining trial bonus is forfeited after liquidation.

Example

Principal 2000U + Bonus 500U
When opening a position of 1300U:

Bonus: 500U
Principal: 800U

🔻 When a loss of 1000U occurs,
Bonus deducted: Approximately 384U
Remaining  Approximately 116U → Automatically expires

🔺 When a profit of 600U occurs,

A portion of the commission is deducted as a bonus.

The remaining bonus → Fully expires.

② Position < 500U (small position)

System Rules:

Only a portion of the bonus is used.
Unused bonus is retained.
Losses are shared in the ratio of bonus + principal.
When profits are made, commissions are deducted first.

Example: Principal 2,000U + Bonus 500U
When a position of 500U is opened:

Bonus used: 250U
Principal used: 250U
Remaining bonus: 250U (reserved)

🔻 When a loss of 300U occurs,
Bonus deducted: 150U
Principal deducted: 150U
Remaining 100U → expires.
Remaining 250U bonus → Can be used continuously.

(※ Fees deducted from the experience bonuses are not included in the rebate calculation.)

 Guide to Bonus Usage Rules
Summary of Key Rules

1️⃣ Position ≥ 500U:
The entire bonus is used; any unused portion is automatically forfeited after liquidation.

2️⃣ Position < 500U:
Partial bonus is used; any unused portion can be used for future trades.

3️⃣ The bonus can only be deducted from losses and fees; it does not apply to profits.

① Position ≥ 500U (Large Position)

System Rules:

Full bonus must be used.

Losses are deducted based on the position ratio. Only fees are deducted as a trial bonus for profits. The remaining trial bonus is forfeited after liquidation.

Example

Principal 2000U + Bonus 500U
When opening a position of 1300U:

Bonus: 500U
Principal: 800U

🔻 When a loss of 1000U occurs,
Bonus deducted: Approximately 384U
Remaining  Approximately 116U → Automatically expires

🔺 When a profit of 600U occurs,

A portion of the commission is deducted as a bonus.

The remaining bonus → Fully expires.

② Position < 500U (small position)

System Rules:

Only a portion of the bonus is used.
Unused bonus is retained.
Losses are shared in the ratio of bonus + principal.
When profits are made, commissions are deducted first.

Example: Principal 2,000U + Bonus 500U
When a position of 500U is opened:

Bonus used: 250U
Principal used: 250U
Remaining bonus: 250U (reserved)

🔻 When a loss of 300U occurs,
Bonus deducted: 150U
Principal deducted: 150U
Remaining 100U → expires.
Remaining 250U bonus → Can be used continuously.

please send your information if you join this event

 Guide to Bonus Usage Rules
Summary of Key Rules

1️⃣ Position ≥ 500U:
The entire bonus is used; any unused portion is automatically forfeited after liquidation.

2️⃣ Position < 500U:
Partial bonus is used; any unused portion can be used for future trades.

3️⃣ The bonus can only be deducted from losses and fees; it does not apply to profits.

① Position ≥ 500U (Large Position)

System Rules:

Full bonus must be used.

Losses are deducted based on the position ratio. Only fees are deducted as a trial bonus for profits. The remaining trial bonus is forfeited after liquidation.

Example

Principal 2000U + Bonus 500U
When opening a position of 1300U:

Bonus: 500U
Principal: 800U

🔻 When a loss of 1000U occurs,
Bonus deducted: Approximately 384U
Remaining  Approximately 116U → Automatically expires

🔺 When a profit of 600U occurs,

A portion of the commission is deducted as a bonus.

The remaining bonus → Fully expires.

System Rules:

Unused bonus is retained.

Remaining bonus: 250U (reserved)
